behavior find_food_bread_2084_around_fridge_126(food_bread:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_bread)
    body:
        assert is_food_bread(food_bread)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==126
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_bread,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_bread,fridge_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_bread]=False
        close[food_bread,fridge_instance]=True
        close[fridge_instance,food_bread]=True

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_in_trash(item: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_bread_2084_around_fridge_126(food_bread:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_bread)
    body:
        assert is_food_bread(food_bread)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==126
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_bread,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_bread,fridge_instance)

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trashcan(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select a fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trashcan

        foreach item: item:
            # Throw all items from the fridge into the trashcan
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_items_in_trashcan(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_bread_2084_around_fridge_126(food_bread:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_bread)
    body:
        assert is_food_bread(food_bread)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==126
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_into_trashcan(item: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                # If the item is inside the fridge, throw it into the trashcan
                throw_item_into_trashcan(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_bread_2084_around_fridge_126(food_bread:item):

            exp(food_bread,fridge_instance)
        else:

behavior find_food_rice_2108_around_fridge_126(food_rice:item):

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_to_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Iterate over all items in the fridge
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                bind trashcan: item where:
                    is_trashcan(trashcan)
                # Select a trashcan
                throw_to_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_each_item_to_trashcan(o: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(o, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan

        foreach o: item:
            if inside(o, fridge):
                throw_each_item_to_trashcan(o, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation

behavior remove_from_fridge(item:item, fridge:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, fridge)
        # Temporarily remove the item from the fridge

behavior throw_away(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        # Put the item into the trashcan

behavior handle_items_from_fridge(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge) and not is_trashcan(item):
                remove_from_fridge(item, fridge)
                throw_away(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        handle_items_from_fridge(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

Reset goals: The sub-goals are: 
['Throw all the items in the fridge to the trashcan.']

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trash(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        throw_items_in_trash(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan) 

behavior find_trash_can():
    body:
        foreach trashcan: item:
            if is_trashcan(trashcan) and not visited(trashcan):
                observe(trashcan,"Check if it is accessible")

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_items_in_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
def is_inside_fridge(fridge:item, item:item):
    # Function to check if an item is inside the fridge
    return inside(item, fridge)

behavior throw_to_trash_can(item:item, trash_can:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trash_can)
        # Place the item inside the trash can

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        
        bind trash_can: item where:
            is_trashcan(trash_can)
        # Select the trash can

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):  # Identify items inside the fridge
                throw_to_trash_can(item, trash_can)
                # Throw each item in the fridge to the trash can

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trash(x:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(x, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_items_in_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

behavior throw_item_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select a fridge
        
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                # Identify all items inside the fridge
                bind trashcan: item where:
                    is_trashcan(trashcan)
                # Select a trash can
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)
                # Throw each item found in the fridge into the trash can

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_in_trashcan(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior process_item_in_fridge(item:item, fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        if is_food(item):
            bind trashcan: item where:
                is_trashcan(trashcan)
            throw_in_trashcan(item, trashcan)
        else:
            # Handle nonfood items if necessary

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                process_item_in_fridge(item, fridge, trashcan)


#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation

behavior throw_item_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior throw_all_items_in_trashcan(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        throw_all_items_in_trashcan(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_in_trashcan(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trashcan

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trashcan(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
def has_items_in_fridge(fridge:item):
    # Function to check if there are items inside the fridge
    symbol has_items= exists o: item : (inside(o, fridge))
    return has_items

behavior throw_away(items:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(items, trashcan)
        # Throw the item into the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge) 

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)

        if has_items_in_fridge(fridge):
            foreach items: item:
                if inside(items, fridge):
                    throw_away(items, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_in_trash(item: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)


#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trash(obj: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(obj, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        
        foreach obj: item:
            if inside(obj, fridge):
                throw_items_in_trash(obj, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end
